		}
	}

	8068.1.1 = {add_spouse=45159}
	8110.1.1 = { add_trait=blinded_age }
	8129.4.1={ #Dance of the Dragons
		effect = {
			set_character_flag = neutral
			clr_character_flag = supporting_king
			clr_character_flag = against_king
			set_defacto_liege=THIS
			any_vassal = { 
				set_character_flag = neutral
				clr_character_flag = supporting_king
				clr_character_flag = against_king
			}
			e_iron_throne = {
				holder_scope = { 
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_dithered
						who = ROOT
						years = 5
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	8130.3.5 = {death="8130.3.5"}
}

14159 = {
	name="Hodor"	# Father of Kermit Tully, Lord of Riverrun during dance
	dynasty=159
	
	stewardship=8

	religion="the_seven"
	culture="riverlander"

	father=154159
	mother=454159
	
	add_trait=stubborn
	add_trait=wroth
	add_trait=authoritative

	8090.1.1 = {birth="8090.1.1"}
	8106.1.1 = {add_trait=knight add_trait=skilled_warrior}
	8112.1.1 = {add_spouse=44159}
	8130.3.5 = {
		effect = {
			clr_character_flag = against_king
			any_vassal = { clr_character_flag = against_king }
			set_defacto_liege=THIS
			e_iron_throne = {
				holder_scope = { 
					remove_opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_joined_rebellion
						who = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			d_dragonstone = {
				holder_scope = { 
					remove_opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = opinion_joined_cause
					}
					reverse_remove_opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader
						who = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	8130.4.14 = {add_trait= ill death = {death_reason = death_trait}} # Died of an Illness
}

14140 = {
	name="Hodor"
	dynasty=140
	
	religion="the_seven"
	culture="riverlander"
	
	father=15140
	
	8019.1.1 = {birth="8019.1.1"}
	8043.1.1={ #Faith Militant Uprising
		effect = {
			set_defacto_liege = ROOT
			set_character_flag = against_king
			any_demesne_title = {
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						tier = COUNT
						tier = DUKE
					}
				}				
				set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 3 } #riverlands
			}
			e_iron_throne = {
				holder_scope = { 
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_joined_rebellion
						who = ROOT
						years = 20
					}
				}
			}
			k_the_most_devout = {
				holder_scope = { 
					opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = opinion_joined_cause
					}
					reverse_opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader
						who = ROOT
						years = 100
					}
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { year = 8197 } }
						ROOT = {
							join_attacker_wars = PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	8044.1.1={ 
		effect = {
			k_riverlands = {
				holder_scope = {
					ROOT = { set_defacto_liege = PREV }
				}
			}
			clr_character_flag = against_king
			
			e_iron_throne = {
				holder_scope = { 
					remove_opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_joined_rebellion
						who = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			k_the_most_devout = {
				holder_scope = { 
					remove_opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = opinion_joined_cause
					}
					reverse_remove_opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader
						who = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	8059.1.1 = {death="8059.1.1"}

1001438 = {
	name="Hodor"
	dynasty=1438

	religion="the_seven"
	culture="riverlander"

	father=2001438
	
	8173.1.1 = {birth="8173.1.1"}
	8195.3.7={ #Blackfyre Rebellion
		raise_levies = {
			location = 92 #Bluefork
			force_mult = 1
		}
		effect = {
			set_defacto_liege = ROOT
			set_character_flag = against_king
			set_character_flag = against_loyal_liege
			any_demesne_title = {
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						tier = COUNT
						tier = DUKE
					}
				}				
				set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 3 } #riverlands
			}
			e_iron_throne = {
				holder_scope = { 
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_joined_rebellion
						who = ROOT
						years = 20
					}
				}
			}
			d_daemon_blackfyres_host = {
				holder_scope = { 
					opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = opinion_joined_cause
					}
					reverse_opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader
						who = ROOT
						years = 100
					}
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { year = 8197 } }
						ROOT = {
							join_attacker_wars = PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	8196.12.31={ 
		effect = {
			k_riverlands = {
				holder_scope = {
					ROOT = { set_defacto_liege = PREV }
				}
			}
			clr_character_flag = against_king
			clr_character_flag = against_loyal_liege
			e_iron_throne = {
				holder_scope = { 
					remove_opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_joined_rebellion
						who = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			d_daemon_blackfyres_host = {
				holder_scope = { 
					remove_opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = opinion_joined_cause
					}
					reverse_remove_opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader
						who = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	8201.1.1 = {death="8201.1.1"}
}
